1. **Current State Analysis**:
   - **Victory Points**: You have 1 victory point from your initial settlement at node 40.
   - **Resources**: You have no resources currently.

     - â›ï¸ Ore from the tile at (-2, 2, 0) with a dice roll of 11.
     - ğŸŒ¾ Wheat from the tile at (-1, 2, -1) with a dice roll of 6.
   - This means you are likely to collect Ore and Wheat effectively.

3. **Available Actions**:
   - [0] Build a road at edge (40, 42)
   - [1] Build a road at edge (40, 44)
   - [2] Build a road at edge (18, 40)

4. **Strategic Considerations**:
   - **Resource Collection**: Building a road towards a port can help with resource trading.
   - **Future Settlements**: Building towards nodes that can become future settlements is crucial.
   - **Development Cards**: Accessing ports can help trade for development cards.

5. **Immediate and Future Benefits**:
   - Building a road at edge (40, 44) gives you access to the 2:1 Wood Port, which can be beneficial for trading Wood.
   - Building a road at edge (40, 42) does not provide immediate port access but can be part of a longer strategy.
   - Building a road at edge (18, 40) connects to the Wheat resource tile, which can be beneficial for future settlements.

6. **Decision**:
   - Building a road at edge (40, 44) provides immediate access to the Wood Port, which can be strategically beneficial for future trades and resource management.
